## Brand Guidelines

### 2013

**Logo Information:**

- Reference to Samsung logo usage, including its branding on products and endtags.

**Color Information:**

- Symbols use Sky Blue as the primary color, with gradients for depth and motion. Secondary colors include Ivy, Berry, Sun, Lotus, Plum, and Coal in various tones (55%, 80%, 100%).

**Typography Information:**

- 16pt Arial Regular is used for email signatures; colors used include Grey RGB 117/120/123 and Blue RGB 6/137/216.
- For Word Frames, 'Samsung Interface Black' is the typeface, and tracking is set to -100 with kerning adjustments for legibility. Refer to typography guidance for additional details.

**Imagery Photography:**

- Guidance on using lifestyle photography layered with frames (Product, Simple, and Word) to emphasize discovery and engagement. Careful composition includes Gaussian blur and positioning.

**Spacing Layout:**

- Clear space rules for frame layouts require proper spacing between elements such as the product frames and product names in communication materials.
- General layout structure emphasizes layers: Message layer (containing the Samsung wordmark, headlines, and body text), Discovery layer (product frames), and Possibility layer (photography). 10° acceleration angle is a guideline.

**Brand Voice:**

- Messaging focuses on clear, inviting communication of Samsung's innovative products and features. This is reflected through design elements like Word Frames and lifestyle imagery.

**Notes:**

- Frames and layout matrices vary by product category (e.g., mobile layouts, refrigerator layouts, camera layouts). Detailed layout matrices available for specific devices.
- The Samsung 'Planet First' logo integrates Samsung Interface typography with the primary and secondary color palette to reflect brand sustainability ethos.
- Symbols used to communicate product features should have a coherent family style and can use primary or secondary colors for dynamic or feature-specific applications.
